<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>

<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>
<s> here in the luncheon interval were all species of female and one species of male hat protecting the multiple types of face associated with the classes <\s>
<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>
<s> something wonderfully uplifting and reassuring in that query and the sight of so many people like themselves voicing it <\s>
<s> what reserve power in the british realm enough pigeons lobsters lamb salmon mayonnaise strawberries and bottles of champagne to feed the lot <\s>

<s> wars might rage taxation prey trades unions take toll and europe perish of starvation but the ten thousand would be fed and within their ring fence stroll upon green turf wear their top hats and meet themselves <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>
<s> here in the luncheon interval were all species of female and one species of male hat protecting the multiple types of face associated with the classes <\s>
<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>
<s> here in the luncheon interval were all species of female and one species of male hat protecting the multiple types of face associated with the classes <\s>
<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>
<s> here in the luncheon interval were all species of female and one species of male hat protecting the multiple types of face associated with the classes <\s>
<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>
<s> something wonderfully uplifting and reassuring in that query and the sight of so many people like themselves voicing it <\s>

<s> he supposed that people drank too much still but there was not the scope for it there used to be <\s>

<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>
<s> something wonderfully uplifting and reassuring in that query and the sight of so many people like themselves voicing it <\s>
<s> what reserve power in the british realm enough pigeons lobsters lamb salmon mayonnaise strawberries and bottles of champagne to feed the lot <\s>
<s> no miracle in prospect no case of seven loaves and a few fishes faith rested on surer foundations <\s>

<s> how strong and how elastic <\s>
<s> wars might rage taxation prey trades unions take toll and europe perish of starvation but the ten thousand would be fed and within their ring fence stroll upon green turf wear their top hats and meet themselves <\s>
<s> the heart was sound the pulse still regular <\s>
<s> among the many forsytes present on a hunting ground theirs by personal prescriptive right or proxy was soames with his wife and daughter <\s>

<s> he remembered suddenly with what intoxication of pride he had walked round with irene in the first years of his first marriage <\s>
<s> and how they used to lunch on the drag which his mother would make his father have because it was so chic all drags and carriages in those days not these lumbering great stands <\s>
<s> and how consistently montague dartie had drunk too much <\s>
<s> he supposed that people drank too much still but there was not the scope for it there used to be <\s>

<s> among the many forsytes present on a hunting ground theirs by personal prescriptive right or proxy was soames with his wife and daughter <\s>

<s> he supposed that people drank too much still but there was not the scope for it there used to be <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>

<s> xi timothy prophesies on the day of the cancelled meeting at the national gallery began the second anniversary of the resurrection of england's pride and glory or more shortly the top hat <\s>
<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>

<s> lord's that festival which the war had driven from the field raised its light and dark blue flags for the second time displaying almost every feature of a glorious past <\s>
<s> here in the luncheon interval were all species of female and one species of male hat protecting the multiple types of face associated with the classes <\s>
<s> the observing forsyte might discern in the free or unconsidered seats a certain number of the squash hatted but they hardly ventured on the grass the old school or schools could still rejoice that the proletariat was not yet paying the necessary half crown <\s>
<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>
<s> something wonderfully uplifting and reassuring in that query and the sight of so many people like themselves voicing it <\s>
<s> what reserve power in the british realm enough pigeons lobsters lamb salmon mayonnaise strawberries and bottles of champagne to feed the lot <\s>
<s> no miracle in prospect no case of seven loaves and a few fishes faith rested on surer foundations <\s>

<s> there was life in the old dog yet <\s>
<s> how strong and how elastic <\s>
<s> wars might rage taxation prey trades unions take toll and europe perish of starvation but the ten thousand would be fed and within their ring fence stroll upon green turf wear their top hats and meet themselves <\s>
<s> the heart was sound the pulse still regular <\s>
<s> among the many forsytes present on a hunting ground theirs by personal prescriptive right or proxy was soames with his wife and daughter <\s>
<s> he had not been at either school he took no interest in cricket but he wanted fleur to show her frock and he wanted to wear his top hat parade it again in peace and plenty among his peers <\s>
<s> he walked sedately with fleur between him and annette <\s>
<s> no women equalled them so far as he could see <\s>
<s> they could walk and hold themselves up there was substance in their good looks the modern woman had no build no chest no anything <\s>
<s> he remembered suddenly with what intoxication of pride he had walked round with irene in the first years of his first marriage <\s>
<s> and how they used to lunch on the drag which his mother would make his father have because it was so chic all drags and carriages in those days not these lumbering great stands <\s>
<s> and how consistently montague dartie had drunk too much <\s>
<s> he supposed that people drank too much still but there was not the scope for it there used to be <\s>
<s> he remembered george forsyte whose brothers roger and eustace had been at harrow and eton towering up on the top of the drag waving a light blue flag with one hand and a dark blue flag with the other and shouting etroow harrton <\s>
<s> just when everybody was silent like the buffoon he had always been and eustace got up to the nines below too dandified to wear any colour or take any notice <\s>

<s> here was still a close borough the only one left on a large scale for the papers were about to estimate the attendance at ten thousand <\s>
<s> and the ten thousand all animated by one hope were asking each other one question where are you lunching <\s>
<s> something wonderfully uplifting and reassuring in that query and the sight of so many people like themselves voicing it <\s>

<s> among the many forsytes present on a hunting ground theirs by personal prescriptive right or proxy was soames with his wife and daughter <\s>

<s> he supposed that people drank too much still but there was not the scope for it there used to be <\s>

<s> but the war of motives within him was but postponed the longing for fleur and the hatred of deception <\s>
<s> he came to the old chalk pit above wansdon with his mind no more made up than when he started <\s>

<s> his things had already been brought up <\s>
